				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Die Ruinen von Athen, Op.113 (Beethoven, Ludwig van)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>9 sections
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1811 (and 1822)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Incidental_music&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Incidental music</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Theatrical_Works&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Theatrical Works</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_3_voices%2C_mixed_chorus%2C_orchestra&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For 3 voices, mixed chorus, orchestra</a></span>; <span class="expandline" title="24 more..."><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_voices_and_chorus_with_orchestra&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For voices and chorus with orchestra</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_voice&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the voice</a></span>; <tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Die Ruinen von Athen
</td></tr>

<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="zh-hans, zh">雅典的废墟</span>; <span title="zh-hant, zh-hk">雅典的廢墟</span>; <span title="ja">アテネの廃墟</span>; <span title="fr">Les Ruines d'Athènes</span>; <span title="ca">Les ruïnes d'Atenes</span>; <span class="expandline" title="2 more..."><span title="sv">Athens ruiner</span>; <span title="pl">Ruiny Aten</span></span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Aliases
</th>

</td></tr>

<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>9 sections (including overture)
<dl><dd>Overture. Andante con moto, (G&#160;minor) - Allegro, ma non troppo (G&#160;major)
</dd><dd>1. Chor. Andante poco sostenuto (E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</dd><dd>2. Duett. Andante con moto - Poco piu mosso, (G&#160;minor)
</dd><dd>3. Chor. Allegro ma non troppo (G major)
</dd><dd>4. Marcia alla turca. Vivace (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</dd><dd>5. Musick hinter der Scene. Allegro assai ma non troppo (C&#160;major)
</dd><dd>6. Marsch und chor. Assai moderato (E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major) Op.114
</dd><dd>6a. Recitativo. Vivace (G&#160;major)
</dd><dd>7a. Chor. Allegretto ma non troppo (G&#160;major)
</dd><dd>7b. Aria mit Chor. Adagio - Allegro con brio (C&#160;major)
</dd><dd>8. Chor. Allegro con fuoco (A&#160;major)
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Text Incipit
</th>
<td><i>see below</i>
<dl><dd>1. Tochter des mächtigen Zeus
</dd><dd>2. Ohne Verschulden Knechtschaft dulden
</dd><dd>3. Du hast in deines Ärmels Falten
</dd><dd>6. Schmückt die Altare
</dd><dd>6a. Mit reger Freude 
</dd><dd>7a. Wir tragen empfängliche Herzen im Busen
</dd><dd>7b.Will unser Genius noch einen Wunsch gewähren?
<dl><dd>Er ist's! Wir sind erhört!
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>8. Heil unserm König!
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
